                         Authentic Mid Century decor with colorful modern flair. Our 1969 home has retro art &amp; furnishings. Easy 110/405 freeway access to all parts of Los Angeles &amp; Orange County. Relax in our master bedroom w/private bath &amp; balcony with cool ocean breezes.

                        <div data-reactid="619">
                         Welcome to the best hidden Mid-Century Modern gem in Los Angeles! We nicknamed our home "The Dream Chasers' Retreat" for the guests we meet who visit and move to Los Angeles pursuing a dream. This city is full of amazing, creative visitors and locals who dream big. We are offering a modern, calming master bedroom with an amazing 260 degree view around the South Bay from the private balcony. The bright private en-suite bathroom has a lovely walk in shower. The bed is a comfortable queen size bed. This room is the master bedroom in The Dream Chaser's Retreat.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="620">
                         Our lovely home is in Harbor City, the southern most part of Los Angeles. This is 1 block east of Torrance and 2 miles from Redondo Beach. It is a safe, tranquil and quiet neighborhood. Most residents enjoy walking their dogs and getting outside to exercise daily. This neighborhood was built in 1969, when Mid-Century Modern met 1970s Retro designs. Within a 15-20 minute drive is Redondo Beach, Torrance Beach, San Pedro and Downtown Long Beach. Popular local destinations nearby are: - Redondo Beach Pier seafood bars &amp; restaurants, plus stunning sunsets - Torrance Beach bike path - Palos Verdes' cliff hiking to tide pools - Long Beach's Convention Center - San Pedro Cruise Warf &amp; Ports-O-Call - Old Town Torrance charm When eating out, our home is convenient to many different types of food: - Korean markets, BBQ &amp; Tofu House - Hawaiian restaurants - Japanese markets, bakeries, Ramen &amp; Sushi - Traditional American breakfast cafes - Asian Fusion restaurants (eg: Peruvian-Japanese, Chinese-Peruvian, Korean-Chinese) Across the street, Mulligans Family Fun is a great place for mini-golf/arcades. It's a one-of-a-kind experience staying at our colorful home.

                         <li data-reactid="1256"><p data-reactid="1257">This is my first AirBnB review so I hope that more experienced users will indulge my minor departures from the usual review parameters. You see, my review of the Beautiful Master Suite is dependent on my impressions of AirBnB, and, likewise, my thoughts on AirBnB are limited to my experience at the Beautiful Master Suite. In my opinion, the most important reason to stay at an AirBnB is the Host. In this specific case, the Catena family (Jodi and Steve and family) is the best reason to recommend the “Beautiful Master Suite” in Torrance, CA. Sure, price is important. But, the whole pricing structure of AirBnB presupposes that the cost will be a much better value than comparable motels and hotels. Don’t take my word for it; make your own price comparisons. I found the Beautiful Master Suite to be about half the price of a similar commercial room. And, location is very important. Location isn’t just geographical positioning. It encompasses access, proximity, noise level, and safety. More often than not, access will be easier at a commercial location right on a busy thoroughfare. Proximity is absolutely dependent on where the traveler needs to be. Noise level and safety must be vetted for each locale. For my purposes, access and proximity to my needs were just right at the Beautiful Master Suite. Noise level was far better than any room on a major boulevard. Safety? You would have to be in a gated community to get any safer. This is Torrance, after all! So, that brings us back to the Catenas -- Jodi, Steve, and family. I can’t imagine a better home to stay in than theirs. Jodi, with her never ending warm smile, Steve with gracious generosity and financial advice, and the kids, with their welcoming patience and endurance, all make a splendid family atmosphere to embrace. They each taught me a little something about family. Specifics? Sure! How about the functional and free workspace -- complete with computer, internet, scanner/copier and printer! And the exquisite décor with maroon and gold throughout and crown moulding above. Least not, the bed was about as comfy as any I’ve had in the most expensive hotels! Entertainment?
